# TS Interface Generator

> Export JSII Compatible Interface from external packages

This repository is an exploration of generating JSII Compatible Interfaces for public packages on NPM.

It has only been tested with the DataDog Typescript API Client package and is not intended for production use.

## Usage

```bash
# install pj dependencies
yarn
# run the export-datadog-interfaces task
npx projen@latest export-datadog-interfaces
# confirm JSII compile works
npx projen@latest compile
```

## How it works

The `export-datadog-interfaces` task uses the `ts-morph` package to parse the DataDog Typescript API Client package and generate a JSII compatible interface for a specific class within the package. It resolves imports and combines all dependencies into a single Typescript source file.

Notes:

- The DataDog API Typescript Client is autogenerated by OpenAPI generator and creates `class` objects only.
- Internal properties such as `attributeTypeMap` are filtered out.
- The `UnparsedObject` type's `_data` property is tagged as internal.

## References

- [Generate RunTypes from TS](https://gist.github.com/skurfuerst/a07ab23c3e40a45f2268f7700ceeceaf)
- [Type FootPrint](https://gist.github.com/zaripych/963fa6584524e5b446b70548dbabbf65)

```typescript

const alertGraphWidgetDefinition: AlertGraphWidgetDefinition = { ... }
```

```typescript
public readonly reflowType: UnparsedObject | string;
```

- *Type:* <a href="#ts-interface-generator.UnparsedObject">UnparsedObject</a> | string

Reflow type for a **new dashboard layout** dashboard.

Set this only when layout type is 'ordered'.
If set to 'fixed', the dashboard expects all widgets to have a layout, and if it's set to 'auto',
widgets should not have layouts.

A list of role identifiers.

Only the author and users associated with at least one of these roles can edit this dashboard.

This property is deprecated; please use the [Restriction Policies API](https://docs.datadoghq.com/api/latest/restriction-policies/) instead to manage write authorization for individual dashboards.


- *Type:* string[]

```typescript
public readonly prefix: string;
```

- *Type:* string

The tag prefix associated with the variable.

Only tags with this prefix appear in the variable drop-down.

### GeomapWidgetDefinition <a name="GeomapWidgetDefinition" id="ts-interface-generator.GeomapWidgetDefinition"></a>

#### Initializer <a name="Initializer" id="ts-interface-generator.GeomapWidgetDefinition.Initializer"></a>

```typescript

```

#### Properties <a name="Properties" id="Properties"></a>

| **Name** | **Type** | **Description** |
| --- | --- | --- |
| <code><a href="#ts-interface-generator.GeomapWidgetDefinition.property.requests">requests</a></code> | <code><a href="#ts-interface-generator.GeomapWidgetRequest">GeomapWidgetRequest</a>[]</code> | Array of one request object to display in the widget. |
| <code><a href="#ts-interface-generator.GeomapWidgetDefinition.property.style">style</a></code> | <code><a href="#ts-interface-generator.GeomapWidgetDefinitionStyle">GeomapWidgetDefinitionStyle</a></code> | The style to apply to the widget. |
| <code><a href="#ts-interface-generator.GeomapWidgetDefinition.property.type">type</a></code> | <code><a href="#ts-interface-generator.UnparsedObject">UnparsedObject</a> \| string</code> | Type of the geomap widget. |
| <code><a href="#ts-interface-generator.GeomapWidgetDefinition.property.view">view</a></code> | <code><a href="#ts-interface-generator.GeomapWidgetDefinitionView">GeomapWidgetDefinitionView</a></code> | The view of the world that the map should render. |
| <code><a href="#ts-interface-generator.GeomapWidgetDefinition.property.customLinks">customLinks</a></code> | <code><a href="#ts-interface-generator.WidgetCustomLink">WidgetCustomLink</a>[]</code> | A list of custom links. |
| <code><a href="#ts-interface-generator.GeomapWidgetDefinition.property.time">time</a></code> | <code><a href="#ts-interface-generator.WidgetTime">WidgetTime</a></code> | Time setting for the widget. |
| <code><a href="#ts-interface-generator.GeomapWidgetDefinition.property.title">title</a></code> | <code>string</code> | The title of your widget. |
| <code><a href="#ts-interface-generator.GeomapWidgetDefinition.property.titleAlign">titleAlign</a></code> | <code><a href="#ts-interface-generator.UnparsedObject">UnparsedObject</a> \| string</code> | How to align the text on the widget. |
| <code><a href="#ts-interface-generator.GeomapWidgetDefinition.property.titleSize">titleSize</a></code> | <code>string</code> | The size of the title. |

---

##### `requests`<sup>Required</sup> <a name="requests" id="ts-interface-generator.GeomapWidgetDefinition.property.requests"></a>

```typescript
public readonly requests: GeomapWidgetRequest[];
```

- *Type:* <a href="#ts-interface-generator.GeomapWidgetRequest">GeomapWidgetRequest</a>[]

Array of one request object to display in the widget.

The request must contain a `group-by` tag whose value is a country ISO code.

See the [Request JSON schema documentation](https://docs.datadoghq.com/dashboards/graphing_json/request_json)
for information about building the `REQUEST_SCHEMA`.

---

##### `style`<sup>Required</sup> <a name="style" id="ts-interface-generator.GeomapWidgetDefinition.property.style"></a>

```typescript
public readonly style: GeomapWidgetDefinitionStyle;
```

- *Type:* <a href="#ts-interface-generator.GeomapWidgetDefinitionStyle">GeomapWidgetDefinitionStyle</a>

The style to apply to the widget.

---

##### `type`<sup>Required</sup> <a name="type" id="ts-interface-generator.GeomapWidgetDefinition.property.type"></a>

```typescript
public readonly type: UnparsedObject | string;
```

- *Type:* <a href="#ts-interface-generator.UnparsedObject">UnparsedObject</a> | string

Type of the geomap widget.

---

##### `time`<sup>Optional</sup> <a name="time" id="ts-interface-generator.GeomapWidgetDefinition.property.time"></a>

```typescript
public readonly queries: UnparsedObject | FormulaAndFunctionMetricQueryDefinition | FormulaAndFunctionEventQueryDefinition | FormulaAndFunctionProcessQueryDefinition | FormulaAndFunctionApmDependencyStatsQueryDefinition | FormulaAndFunctionApmResourceStatsQueryDefinition | FormulaAndFunctionSLOQueryDefinition | FormulaAndFunctionCloudCostQueryDefinition[];
```

- *Type:* <a href="#ts-interface-generator.UnparsedObject">UnparsedObject</a> | <a href="#ts-interface-generator.FormulaAndFunctionMetricQueryDefinition">FormulaAndFunctionMetricQueryDefinition</a> | <a href="#ts-interface-generator.FormulaAndFunctionEventQueryDefinition">FormulaAndFunctionEventQueryDefinition</a> | <a href="#ts-interface-generator.FormulaAndFunctionProcessQueryDefinition">FormulaAndFunctionProcessQueryDefinition</a> | <a href="#ts-interface-generator.FormulaAndFunctionApmDependencyStatsQueryDefinition">FormulaAndFunctionApmDependencyStatsQueryDefinition</a> | <a href="#ts-interface-generator.FormulaAndFunctionApmResourceStatsQueryDefinition">FormulaAndFunctionApmResourceStatsQueryDefinition</a> | <a href="#ts-interface-generator.FormulaAndFunctionSLOQueryDefinition">FormulaAndFunctionSLOQueryDefinition</a> | <a href="#ts-interface-generator.FormulaAndFunctionCloudCostQueryDefinition">FormulaAndFunctionCloudCostQueryDefinition</a>[]

List of queries that can be returned directly or used in formulas.

---

##### `responseFormat`<sup>Optional</sup> <a name="responseFormat" id="ts-interface-generator.ScatterplotTableRequest.property.responseFormat"></a>

```typescript
public readonly responseFormat: UnparsedObject | string;
```

- *Type:* <a href="#ts-interface-generator.UnparsedObject">UnparsedObject</a> | string

Timeseries, scalar, or event list response.

Event list response formats are supported by Geomap widgets.

#### Properties <a name="Properties" id="Properties"></a>

| **Name** | **Type** | **Description** |

### WidgetCustomLink <a name="WidgetCustomLink" id="ts-interface-generator.WidgetCustomLink"></a>

#### Initializer <a name="Initializer" id="ts-interface-generator.WidgetCustomLink.Initializer"></a>

```typescript
import { WidgetCustomLink } from 'ts-interface-generator'

const widgetCustomLink: WidgetCustomLink = { ... }
```

#### Properties <a name="Properties" id="Properties"></a>

| **Name** | **Type** | **Description** |
| --- | --- | --- |
| <code><a href="#ts-interface-generator.WidgetCustomLink.property.isHidden">isHidden</a></code> | <code>boolean</code> | The flag for toggling context menu link visibility. |
| <code><a href="#ts-interface-generator.WidgetCustomLink.property.label">label</a></code> | <code>string</code> | The label for the custom link URL. |
| <code><a href="#ts-interface-generator.WidgetCustomLink.property.link">link</a></code> | <code>string</code> | The URL of the custom link. |
| <code><a href="#ts-interface-generator.WidgetCustomLink.property.overrideLabel">overrideLabel</a></code> | <code>string</code> | The label ID that refers to a context menu link. |

---

##### `isHidden`<sup>Optional</sup> <a name="isHidden" id="ts-interface-generator.WidgetCustomLink.property.isHidden"></a>

```typescript
public readonly isHidden: boolean;
```

- *Type:* boolean

The flag for toggling context menu link visibility.

---

##### `label`<sup>Optional</sup> <a name="label" id="ts-interface-generator.WidgetCustomLink.property.label"></a>

```typescript
public readonly label: string;
```

- *Type:* string

The label for the custom link URL.

Keep the label short and descriptive. Use metrics and tags as variables.

---

##### `link`<sup>Optional</sup> <a name="link" id="ts-interface-generator.WidgetCustomLink.property.link"></a>

```typescript
public readonly link: string;
```

- *Type:* string

The URL of the custom link.

URL must include `http` or `https`. A relative URL must start with `/`.

---

##### `overrideLabel`<sup>Optional</sup> <a name="overrideLabel" id="ts-interface-generator.WidgetCustomLink.property.overrideLabel"></a>

```typescript
public readonly overrideLabel: string;
```

- *Type:* string

The label ID that refers to a context menu link.

Can be `logs`, `hosts`, `traces`, `profiles`, `processes`, `containers`, or `rum`.

---

### WidgetEvent <a name="WidgetEvent" id="ts-interface-generator.WidgetEvent"></a>

#### Initializer <a name="Initializer" id="ts-interface-generator.WidgetEvent.Initializer"></a>

#### Properties <a name="Properties" id="Properties"></a>

| **Name** | **Type** | **Description** |

### WidgetLayout <a name="WidgetLayout" id="ts-interface-generator.WidgetLayout"></a>

#### Initializer <a name="Initializer" id="ts-interface-generator.WidgetLayout.Initializer"></a>

```typescript
import { WidgetLayout } from 'ts-interface-generator'

const widgetLayout: WidgetLayout = { ... }
```

#### Properties <a name="Properties" id="Properties"></a>

| **Name** | **Type** | **Description** |
| --- | --- | --- |
| <code><a href="#ts-interface-generator.WidgetLayout.property.height">height</a></code> | <code>number</code> | The height of the widget. |
| <code><a href="#ts-interface-generator.WidgetLayout.property.width">width</a></code> | <code>number</code> | The width of the widget. |
| <code><a href="#ts-interface-generator.WidgetLayout.property.x">x</a></code> | <code>number</code> | The position of the widget on the x (horizontal) axis. |
| <code><a href="#ts-interface-generator.WidgetLayout.property.y">y</a></code> | <code>number</code> | The position of the widget on the y (vertical) axis. |
| <code><a href="#ts-interface-generator.WidgetLayout.property.isColumnBreak">isColumnBreak</a></code> | <code>boolean</code> | Whether the widget should be the first one on the second column in high density or not. |

---

##### `height`<sup>Required</sup> <a name="height" id="ts-interface-generator.WidgetLayout.property.height"></a>

```typescript
public readonly height: number;
```

- *Type:* number

The height of the widget.

Should be a non-negative integer.

---

##### `width`<sup>Required</sup> <a name="width" id="ts-interface-generator.WidgetLayout.property.width"></a>

```typescript
public readonly width: number;
```

- *Type:* number

The width of the widget.

Should be a non-negative integer.

---

##### `x`<sup>Required</sup> <a name="x" id="ts-interface-generator.WidgetLayout.property.x"></a>

```typescript
public readonly x: number;
```

- *Type:* number

The position of the widget on the x (horizontal) axis.

Should be a non-negative integer.

---

##### `y`<sup>Required</sup> <a name="y" id="ts-interface-generator.WidgetLayout.property.y"></a>

```typescript
public readonly y: number;
```

- *Type:* number

The position of the widget on the y (vertical) axis.

Should be a non-negative integer.

---

##### `isColumnBreak`<sup>Optional</sup> <a name="isColumnBreak" id="ts-interface-generator.WidgetLayout.property.isColumnBreak"></a>

```typescript
public readonly isColumnBreak: boolean;
```

- *Type:* boolean

Whether the widget should be the first one on the second column in high density or not.

**Note**: Only for the **new dashboard layout** and only one widget in the dashboard should have this property set to `true`.

---

### WidgetMarker <a name="WidgetMarker" id="ts-interface-generator.WidgetMarker"></a>

#### Initializer <a name="Initializer" id="ts-interface-generator.WidgetMarker.Initializer"></a>

```typescript
import { WidgetMarker } from 'ts-interface-generator'

const widgetMarker: WidgetMarker = { ... }
```

#### Properties <a name="Properties" id="Properties"></a>

| **Name** | **Type** | **Description** |
| --- | --- | --- |
| <code><a href="#ts-interface-generator.WidgetMarker.property.value">value</a></code> | <code>string</code> | Value to apply. |
| <code><a href="#ts-interface-generator.WidgetMarker.property.displayType">displayType</a></code> | <code>string</code> | Combination of:   - A severity error, warning, ok, or info   - A line type: dashed, solid, or bold In this case of a Distribution widget, this can be set to be `x_axis_percentile`. |
| <code><a href="#ts-interface-generator.WidgetMarker.property.label">label</a></code> | <code>string</code> | Label to display over the marker. |
| <code><a href="#ts-interface-generator.WidgetMarker.property.time">time</a></code> | <code>string</code> | Timestamp for the widget. |

---

##### `value`<sup>Required</sup> <a name="value" id="ts-interface-generator.WidgetMarker.property.value"></a>

```typescript
public readonly value: string;
```

- *Type:* string

Value to apply.

Can be a single value y = 15 or a range of values 0 < y < 10.

---

##### `displayType`<sup>Optional</sup> <a name="displayType" id="ts-interface-generator.WidgetMarker.property.displayType"></a>

```typescript
public readonly displayType: string;
```

- *Type:* string

Combination of:   - A severity error, warning, ok, or info   - A line type: dashed, solid, or bold In this case of a Distribution widget, this can be set to be `x_axis_percentile`.

---

##### `label`<sup>Optional</sup> <a name="label" id="ts-interface-generator.WidgetMarker.property.label"></a>

```typescript
public readonly label: string;
```

- *Type:* string

Label to display over the marker.

---

##### `time`<sup>Optional</sup> <a name="time" id="ts-interface-generator.WidgetMarker.property.time"></a>

```typescript
public readonly time: string;
```

- *Type:* string

Timestamp for the widget.

---
